	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" >Thiago Silva</h1>
	<div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content">
		<div id="siteSub" class="noprint">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		<div id="contentSub2"></div>
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a>
		<div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="mw-parser-output"><div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Brazilian footballer</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">For the Dave &amp; AJ Tracey song, see <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Silva_(song)" title="Thiago Silva (song)">Thiago Silva (song)</a>. For other people with the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Thiago_Silva_(disambiguation)" class="mw-disambig" title="Thiago Silva (disambiguation)">Thiago Silva (disambiguation)</a>.</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Not to be confused with <a href="/wiki/Tiago_Silva_(disambiguation)" class="mw-redirect mw-disambig" title="Tiago Silva (disambiguation)">Tiago Silva</a>.</div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">This name uses <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_name" title="Portuguese name">Portuguese naming customs</a>: the first or maternal <a href="/wiki/Surname" title="Surname">family name</a> is <i>Emiliano</i>&#32;and the second or paternal family name is <i>da Silva</i>.</div>

* Senior club appearances and goals counted for the domestic league only&#32;and correct as of 09:40, 10 February 2021 (UTC)<br />‡ National team caps and goals correct as of 22:53, 17 November 2020 (UTC)</td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Thiago Emiliano da Silva</b> (<span style="font-size:85%;">Brazilian Portuguese:&#160;</span><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Portuguese" title="Help:IPA/Portuguese">[tiau milinu d siwv]</a></span>; born 22 September 1984), commonly known as <b>Thiago Silva</b>, is a Brazilian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_Football" class="mw-redirect" title="Association Football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Defender_(association_football)#Centre-back" title="Defender (association football)">central defender</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and captains the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil national team</a>. Known for his pace, aerial ability and leadership skills, Silva is regarded as one of the best central defenders of his generation.
<sup id="cite_ref-auto_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-auto1_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After moving back to Europe to join <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a> in 2009, Silva established himself as one of the highest rated defenders in the world, winning the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Italian_football_champions" title="List of Italian football champions">Serie A title</a> with the <i>Rossoneri</i> in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_A.C._Milan_season" title="2010–11 A.C. Milan season">2010–11 season</a>. In July 2012, Paris Saint-Germain signed him for a reported €42 million, making him the then second-<a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">most expensive</a> defender in history behind <a href="/wiki/Rio_Ferdinand" title="Rio Ferdinand">Rio Ferdinand</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> With PSG, Silva won a joint-record seven <a href="/wiki/List_of_French_football_champions" title="List of French football champions">Ligue 1 championships</a>, five consecutive (six overall) <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupes de la Ligue</a> and five <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupes de France</a>, as well as leading his team to their first ever <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> final in <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">2020</a>.
</p><p>A full international since 2008 and a non-playing member of their team at the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a>, Silva <a href="/wiki/Captain_(association_football)" title="Captain (association football)">captained</a> Brazil to victory at the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a> and fourth place at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">World Cup a year later</a>, both on home soil. He was also part of their squads for the two <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_Summer_Olympics" title="Football at the Summer Olympics">Olympic tournaments</a> – winning a <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2008_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2008 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">bronze in 2008</a> and <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2012 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">silver four years later</a> – and three <a href="/wiki/Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="Copa América">Copa América</a> editions, winning the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 edition of the tournament</a> on home soil; overall, he has earned 93 international caps in total.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As a youngster, Silva was admitted into a school in the <a href="/wiki/Campo_Grande,_Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Campo Grande, Rio de Janeiro">Campo Grande</a> neighbourhood of <a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Rio de Janeiro">Rio</a> – coincidentally a feeder school for <a href="/wiki/Fluminense_Football_Club" class="mw-redirect" title="Fluminense Football Club">Fluminense</a>. At the age of 14, Silva impressed Fluminense coach Maurinho during a friendly in <a href="/wiki/Xer%C3%A9m" title="Xerém">Xerém</a>. He was given a short trial, where he was given the role of a defensive midfielder. Silva's playing opportunities were little, prompting him to trial for other clubs. In 1999, at the age of 15, Silva auditioned at <a href="/wiki/Madureira_Esporte_Clube" title="Madureira Esporte Clube">Madureira</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olaria_Esporte_Clube" class="mw-redirect" title="Olaria Esporte Clube">Olaria</a> and <a href="/wiki/Clube_de_Regatas_do_Flamengo" title="Clube de Regatas do Flamengo">Flamengo</a>; he was rejected at each club, the trial at Flamengo being the most difficult for he was not even observed by coaches.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After another unsuccessful trial at <a href="/wiki/Botafogo_de_Futebol_e_Regatas" title="Botafogo de Futebol e Regatas">Botafogo</a>, Silva was taken on by hometown side <a href="/wiki/Barcelona_Esporte_Clube" title="Barcelona Esporte Clube">Barcelona</a>, a small Brazilian club in the lower divisions. The following year, Silva played at a showcase tournament in <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo" title="São Paulo">São Paulo</a> in the hope of attracting attention of bigger clubs. It is there where he was spotted by <a href="/wiki/Paulo_C%C3%A9sar_Carpegiani" title="Paulo César Carpegiani">Paulo César Carpegiani</a>, who invited him to join <a href="/wiki/Pedrabranca_Futebol_Clube" title="Pedrabranca Futebol Clube">RS Futebol</a> in the south of Brazil. Joining the club in the end of 2001, Silva became a professional in 2002 and competed in the <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Ga%C3%BAcho_S%C3%A9rie_B" title="Campeonato Gaúcho Série B">third division of the Campeonato Gaúcho</a>, finishing second and achieving promotion to the state's <a href="/wiki/Campeonato_Ga%C3%BAcho_S%C3%A9rie_A2" title="Campeonato Gaúcho Série A2">second division</a>. In a tournament played in <a href="/wiki/Ancona" title="Ancona">Ancona</a>, Italy, Silva was spotted by <a href="/wiki/Bruno_Conti" title="Bruno Conti">Bruno Conti</a>, a coach with <a href="/wiki/A.S._Roma" title="A.S. Roma">Roma</a>. Conti wanted him to play for Roma, but Silva did not accept the offer.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Strong performances in his last season as a defensive midfielder led to Silva's move to <a href="/wiki/Esporte_Clube_Juventude" title="Esporte Clube Juventude">Juventude</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-globoesporte.globo.com_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-globoesporte.globo.com-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva moved to Juventude in 2004, where he played for six months. At 20 years old, Silva transitioned from midfield to defence under the tutelage of <a href="/wiki/Ivo_Wortmann" title="Ivo Wortmann">Ivo Wortmann</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> In his only season at Juventude, Silva was regarded as the revelation of the season. He was rated by the sports magazine <i><a href="/wiki/Placar" title="Placar">Placar</a></i> as the third-best defender in Brazil, and was included in the team of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Juventude had made a huge leap in league placement during Silva's time at the club – from finishing 18th with 53 points in <a href="/wiki/2003_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="2003 Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">2003</a>, to finishing 7th with 70 points in <a href="/wiki/2004_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="2004 Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">2004</a>. Silva's performances had caught the eye of many clubs with his outstanding performances, and he was sold to <a href="/wiki/FC_Porto" title="FC Porto">Porto</a>.
</p><p>Silva was bought by Porto for €2.5 million in 2004,<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> but played only for the reserve team. After a year in Portugal, he joined <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Moscow" title="FC Dynamo Moscow">Dynamo Moscow</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> where he was diagnosed with <a href="/wiki/Tuberculosis" title="Tuberculosis">tuberculosis</a> and was hospitalised for six months.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> His illness became much worse over time and his doctors told him that if he had been hospitalized two weeks later, he could have died.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> During his recovery, Silva decided to retire from football but was persuaded to reconsider by his mother.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fluminense">Fluminense</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Fluminense">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva returned to football with the help of his former coach, Ivo Wortmann. In 2006, Wortmann was signed as a coach by Fluminense and requested to bring Silva with him, despite Silva's health issues.<sup id="cite_ref-globoesporte.globo.com_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-globoesporte.globo.com-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On 14 January, Fluminense announced the signing of Silva from Porto.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Fluminense struggled in the <a href="/wiki/2006_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="2006 Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">2006 Brasileirão</a>, finishing 15th out of 20 teams; however, Silva was described as one of the best players in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> It is during this time where Silva developed the nickname of "<i>O Monstro</i>" — Portuguese for "The Monster".<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>2007 was a much better year for both Fluminense and for Silva. The club finished in fourth place in the <a href="/wiki/2007_Campeonato_Brasileiro_S%C3%A9rie_A" title="2007 Campeonato Brasileiro Série A">2007 Brasileirão</a>, conceding only 39 goals in 38 matches, enough for the second-best defence in Brazil. More importantly, Fluminense managed a historic victory in the <a href="/wiki/2007_Copa_do_Brasil" title="2007 Copa do Brasil">2007 Copa do Brasil</a>, winning the prestigious trophy for the first time. Silva played a decisive part in the victory; he started in every match, and scored the opening goal in the quarter-final, as well as the equalising goal in the semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Silva's form through the season led him to be selected into <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazilian national team</a> manager <a href="/wiki/Dunga" title="Dunga">Dunga</a>'s preliminary squad for the <a href="/wiki/2007_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2007 Copa América">2007 Copa América</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> After winning the <a href="/wiki/2007_Copa_do_Brasil" title="2007 Copa do Brasil">Copa do Brasil</a>, Silva was recognised by fans as the best defender in Brazil.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, he was one of three nominees for the Best Central Defender award, alongside <a href="/wiki/Breno_Borges" title="Breno Borges">Breno</a> and <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A1bio_Luciano" title="Fábio Luciano">Fábio Luciano</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> The voting results were unveiled on 4 December, where Silva finished second, behind Breno.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceA_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceA-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:15%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Silva is a phenomenon."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Dunga" title="Dunga">Dunga</a>, 2008<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>2008 was a bad year for Fluminense, but Silva's best on an individual level. Having devoted much of their efforts towards the <a href="/wiki/2008_Copa_Libertadores" title="2008 Copa Libertadores">2008 Copa Libertadores</a>, the club's league form suffered, finishing in 14th place. On 18 January, Silva was rewarded by Fluminense's board of directors for his 100th match in the <i>tricolor</i>: He was awarded a shirt with the number "100" and a plaque in honour of his achievements.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Silva became an idol for young Fluminense supporters with his level of performances — the white wristband that Silva would wear during matches became a trend amongst teenagers in Rio de Janeiro who supported the <i>tricolor</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> In May 2008, four fans painted a flag of Silva to honour what they deemed "the best central defender in Brazil". It was first shown in the <a href="/wiki/2008_Copa_Libertadores_knockout_stages#Boca_Juniors_v_Fluminense" title="2008 Copa Libertadores knockout stages">Copa Libertadores semi-final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Boca_Juniors" title="Boca Juniors">Boca Juniors</a><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> — Silva scored a crucial equaliser in the same match.<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was included in the <a href="/wiki/Pr%C3%AAmio_Craque_do_Brasileir%C3%A3o#2008" title="Prêmio Craque do Brasileirão">2008 Brasileirão Team of the Season</a> and was selected as the Fans' Player of the Season.<sup id="cite_ref-Globo_Esporte_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Globo_Esporte-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Silva was widely regarded as one of Fluminense's most important performers in the <a href="/wiki/2008_Copa_Libertadores" title="2008 Copa Libertadores">2008 Copa Libertadores</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-ReferenceB_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ReferenceB-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> reaching the finals only to lose on penalties to <a href="/wiki/LDU_Quito" class="mw-redirect" title="LDU Quito">LDU Quito</a>. Silva's form for Fluminense earned him a call-up to the <i><a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_under-23_football_team" title="Brazil national under-23 football team">Seleção</a></i> to take part in the <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics" title="2008 Summer Olympics">2008 Summer Olympics</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Silva was linked with many clubs in 2008, including the likes of <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and <a href="/wiki/Villarreal_CF" title="Villarreal CF">Villarreal</a>, though ultimately he opted to join the Brazilian contingent already at <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">Milan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> The transfer was confirmed on 12 December.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> In his final match for Fluminense, Silva was cheered by 50,000 supporters who were witnessing his last performance at the <a href="/wiki/Est%C3%A1dio_do_Maracan%C3%A3" class="mw-redirect" title="Estádio do Maracanã">Maracanã</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Milan">Milan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Milan">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>After a five-month chase and a four-hour negotiation period, Silva agreed to a move to Milan for a €10 million fee, with net wages of €2.5 million on a four-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Although Silva could not play competitive matches, he was able to train with the first team. In his first month at Milan, he was taught new defending techniques from <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Maldini" title="Paolo Maldini">Paolo Maldini</a> and manager <a href="/wiki/Carlo_Ancelotti" title="Carlo Ancelotti">Carlo Ancelotti</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Silva played his first match for the <i>Rossoneri</i> in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a> on 21 January 2009; he played well, making ten tackles. His performance drew praise from Milan executive <a href="/wiki/Adriano_Galliani" title="Adriano Galliani">Adriano Galliani</a> and teammate <a href="/wiki/Clarence_Seedorf" title="Clarence Seedorf">Clarence Seedorf</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> Silva was officially registered as a Milan player for the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_A.C._Milan_season" title="2009–10 A.C. Milan season">2009–10 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2009.E2.80.9310_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2009–10_season">2009–10 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2009–10 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva played his first competitive match of the season against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Siena" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Siena">Siena</a> on 22 August 2009. After the match, he was praised for a strong individual performance alongside teammate <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Nesta" title="Alessandro Nesta">Alessandro Nesta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Milan legend Paolo Maldini claimed that Silva had the "physical and technical characteristics of a champion",<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> while Nesta said that Silva would "extend my life as a central defender".<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 23 September, Silva left training with a muscle strain; he was inactive for the next four matches.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> In October, Silva followed a poor performance against Roma<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> with two great displays against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_C.F." class="mw-redirect" title="Real Madrid C.F.">Real Madrid</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Silva also had a wrongly disallowed goal in Milan's away victory.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:29%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Thiago Silva will extend my life as a central defender."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Nesta" title="Alessandro Nesta">Alessandro Nesta</a>, 2009<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 8 November, Silva scored a goal – as well as an own-goal – in a 2–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/S.S._Lazio" title="S.S. Lazio">Lazio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> His quick transition to European football was met with a lot of interest from Italian media — the investment of €10 million to acquire Silva was regarded as a good decision; the <i><a href="/wiki/La_Gazzetta_dello_Sport" title="La Gazzetta dello Sport">La Gazzetta dello Sport</a></i>, the largest daily newspaper in Italy,<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> claimed that Silva's value had doubled at that point.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 25 November, Silva put in a man of the match performance against <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a> to secure passage into the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2009–10 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">knockout stages</a> of the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> In a match against <a href="/wiki/FC_Z%C3%BCrich" title="FC Zürich">Zürich</a> on 8 December, Silva was substituted after 20 minutes with a muscle injury. It was suspected that Silva tore a muscle, and would miss up to two months,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> though after clinical examinations, the injury was found to be a strain rather than a tear.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> On 30 December, Silva was pronounced to be fully fit by club doctor Massimo Manara.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 January 2010, Milan defeated <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> by a score of 3–0;<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Silva was rated as one of the best performers on the day,<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> and <i>La Gazzetta dello Sport</i> compared the understanding of Silva and Nesta to the legendary duo of <a href="/wiki/Franco_Baresi" title="Franco Baresi">Franco Baresi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alessandro_Costacurta" title="Alessandro Costacurta">Alessandro Costacurta</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 15 January, Silva's teammate <a href="/wiki/Alexandre_Pato" title="Alexandre Pato">Alexandre Pato</a> claimed that Silva would become the best defender in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> In a match against <a href="/wiki/Udinese_Calcio" title="Udinese Calcio">Udinese</a> on 12 February, Silva picked up a muscle injury, leaving him in doubt for Milan's upcoming Champions League match against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 6 March, Silva was selected as man of the match in a 0–0 draw with fellow <i><a href="/wiki/Scudetto" title="Scudetto">Scudetto</a></i> challengers Roma.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, Silva was rated as the third-best central defender in the <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Serie_A" title="2009–10 Serie A">2009–10 Serie A</a> by <i>La Gazzetta dello Sport</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2010.E2.80.9311_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010–11_season">2010–11 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2010–11 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva's season began with a goal against <a href="/wiki/U.S._Lecce" title="U.S. Lecce">Lecce</a> in the first match of the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Serie_A" title="2010–11 Serie A">2010–11 Serie A season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> In a 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/A.C._Chievo_Verona" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Chievo Verona">Chievo</a> on 16 October, Silva was forced to leave the match with a sprained left ankle. The injury forced Silva to miss a <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2010–11 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> match against Real Madrid — Milan CEO Adriano Galliani jokingly said after the match that he would give Silva his healthy foot in order to see him play at the <a href="/wiki/Santiago_Bernab%C3%A9u_Stadium" title="Santiago Bernabéu Stadium">Santiago Bernabéu Stadium</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> Silva was inactive for four matches due to his injury. After returning from his injury, he was to play in the <a href="/wiki/Derby_della_Madonnina" title="Derby della Madonnina">Derby della Madonnina</a> against city rivals and <a href="/wiki/Treble_(association_football)" title="Treble (association football)">treble</a> winners Inter Milan. Matched against <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Club Footballer of the Year">UEFA Club Footballer of the Year</a> winner <a href="/wiki/Diego_Milito" title="Diego Milito">Diego Milito</a>, Silva nullified his efforts and played a key role in Milan's 1–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> In a 0–2 group stage loss to <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a> in the Champions League, Silva suffered a right knee injury that required arthroscopic surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Initially feared to be a serious injury,<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> it only kept Silva away for one month.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> At the midpoint of the season, Silva was regarded as the best defender in the <a href="/wiki/Serie_A" title="Serie A">Serie A</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> and the best in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:40%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I think that Thiago Silva is the best defender in the world. It is incredible how good he really is. Thiago Silva is part of a new generation of phenomenal players who are perhaps born once every 100 years."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Filippo_Inzaghi" title="Filippo Inzaghi">Filippo Inzaghi</a>, 2011<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Forced to play as an emergency defensive midfielder due to an injury crisis, Silva played extraordinarily well against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Cesena" title="A.C. Cesena">Cesena</a>, a match which Milan won 2–0. Silva's performance brought comparisons to legendary Milan midfielder <a href="/wiki/Marcel_Desailly" title="Marcel Desailly">Marcel Desailly</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> In his next match, Silva was rated as the best player in Milan's 2–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/U.C._Sampdoria" title="U.C. Sampdoria">Sampdoria</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Coppa_Italia" title="2010–11 Coppa Italia">Coppa Italia quarter-final</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> The midfield "experiment" continued in a 0–0 draw against Lazio, though this time, Silva was compared to another legendary Milan midfielder, <a href="/wiki/Frank_Rijkaard" title="Frank Rijkaard">Frank Rijkaard</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> Silva was lauded by Italian media for his display against <a href="/wiki/S.S.C._Napoli" title="S.S.C. Napoli">Napoli</a>, marking-out star striker <a href="/wiki/Edinson_Cavani" title="Edinson Cavani">Edinson Cavani</a>. Milan won 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> One publication claimed that Silva and Nesta "made a ghost" of Cavani,<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> whereas another claimed that Cavani had a "nightmare".<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the match that sealed the <i>Scudetto</i> for Milan, Silva anchored the <i>Rossoneri</i> to a 3–0 victory in the Derby della Madonnina against city rivals Inter.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the season, Silva extended his contract to June 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> Silva managed to complete the entire <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Serie_A" title="2010–11 Serie A">2010–11 Serie A</a> having earned only one yellow card, and having committed 26 fouls in 33 total matches.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> Silva's individual season was met with praise from all across Europe. In a fan vote, Silva was selected as Milan Player of the Season with 66.6% of the vote.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> <i>La Gazzetta dello Sport</i> rated him as the Player of the Season.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> Silva was selected as Goal's Serie A Player of the Season,<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> and was also voted as the best defender in the league by Italian media and his fellow professionals.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2011.E2.80.9312_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–12_season">2011–12 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2011–12 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg/220px-Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="260" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg/330px-Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg/440px-Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1549" data-file-height="1828" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_silva_4_commons_2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Thiago Silva contesting a ball against <a href="/wiki/A.C._Siena" class="mw-redirect" title="A.C. Siena">Siena</a>, on 17 December 2011</div></div></div>
<p>Milan's season began with a 2–1 victory over Inter in the <a href="/wiki/2011_Supercoppa_Italiana" title="2011 Supercoppa Italiana">2011 Supercoppa Italiana</a>; Silva was the best defender in the match and one of the best overall performers, making a decisive last-man tackle on <a href="/wiki/Samuel_Eto%27o" title="Samuel Eto&#39;o">Samuel Eto'o</a> to deny a clear chance in the first half.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> Milan began the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Serie_A" title="2011–12 Serie A">2011–12 Serie A</a> in poor form, winning only two points in the first three matches, though Silva was one of the better players in the draws against Lazio<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> and Udinese.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> In a <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2011–12 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2011–12 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> match against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, Silva and Alessandro Nesta were crucial in the 2–2 result; both defenders were regarded as two of the best performers by Italian and Catalan media.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> In the match, Silva scored the 90th-minute equaliser — his former coach Carlo Ancelotti predicted that Silva would score that goal.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A knee contusion in a 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/U.S._Citt%C3%A0_di_Palermo" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. Città di Palermo">Palermo</a> on 15 October kept Silva out for two matches.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup> In Silva's 75th Serie A match for Milan, played on 19 November, he was vital in maintaining a clean sheet against <a href="/wiki/ACF_Fiorentina" title="ACF Fiorentina">Fiorentina</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> The next week, Silva was named captain against Chievo, in the process becoming the first foreign captain in 50 years for Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup> In the 4–0 demolition at the <a href="/wiki/San_Siro" title="San Siro">San Siro</a>, Silva scored his first goal as captain, while teammate <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> also scored his 100th Serie A goal in the same match.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> On 1 December, Silva was shortlisted for the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFPro_World_XI" title="FIFPro">FIFPro World XI</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/1994_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1994 FIFA World Cup">1994 World Cup</a>-winning coach <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Alberto_Parreira" title="Carlos Alberto Parreira">Carlos Alberto Parreira</a> regarded Silva as the best Brazilian footballer in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 9 January, Silva was compared to Milan's greatest player,<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Franco Baresi, by his teammate <a href="/wiki/Gennaro_Gattuso" title="Gennaro Gattuso">Gennaro Gattuso</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> On 13 January, Zlatan Ibrahimovi claimed that Silva was the best defender he had ever played with.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> Silva was voted into the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year#Team_of_the_Year_2011" title="UEFA Team of the Year">2011 UEFA Team of the Year</a> on 18 January.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> Silva was selected as man of the match in a 0–0 draw against Napoli in February.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> In Milan's 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2011–12 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League Round of 16</a>, Silva successfully marked-out <a href="/wiki/Robin_van_Persie" title="Robin van Persie">Robin van Persie</a>, who was in a great run of form.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup> Silva played his last full league match for Milan on 17 March against <a href="/wiki/S.S.D._Parma_Calcio_1913" class="mw-redirect" title="S.S.D. Parma Calcio 1913">Parma</a>, playing an important role in the 2–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> Manchester United captain <a href="/wiki/Nemanja_Vidi%C4%87" title="Nemanja Vidi">Nemanja Vidi</a> said that Silva was the best defender in the world in an interview on 22 March.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:35%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"It's difficult to identify where he can still improve. He has already proven to have everything."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Franco_Baresi" title="Franco Baresi">Franco Baresi</a>, 2012<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>On 24 March, Silva was forced out of a match against Roma after ten minutes due to a serious injury. Although Milan originally claimed Silva would be out just four weeks,<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup> instead he missed seven weeks, including the <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_UEFA_Champions_League#Quarter-finals" title="2011–12 UEFA Champions League">Champions League quarter-finals</a> against Barcelona, where Milan fell 1–3 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Without Silva, Milan stuttered in the league and lost the <i>Scudetto</i> to rivals Juventus. It was argued that Silva's injury was the turning point in the title race: with Silva, Milan won 2.37 out of a possible 3 points per match, while without him Milan won 2.09 out of a possible 3 points.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Silva's strong season finished in another nomination to the Serie A Team of the Year, being joint-best central defender alongside Juve stalwart <a href="/wiki/Andrea_Barzagli" title="Andrea Barzagli">Andrea Barzagli</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> He was also regarded as one of the best defenders in Italy by multiple independent publications.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-just-football.com_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-just-football.com-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Paris Saint-Germain">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The negotiations to bring Silva to <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> took place at the end of the 2011–12 season. The saga took over a month to complete. On 11 June 2012, it was reported that Milan legend Paolo Maldini would convince Silva to join PSG in the summer.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> Major French newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/L%27%C3%89quipe" title="L&#39;Équipe">L'Équipe</a></i> claimed that a transfer would be completed by 15 June.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> The same day, PSG sporting director — and former Milan coach — <a href="/wiki/Leonardo_Ara%C3%BAjo" title="Leonardo Araújo">Leonardo</a> officially declared interest in acquiring Silva.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> The next day, however, Milan general director Ariedo Braida claimed that Silva was not for sale.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> On 13 June, Maldini refuted claims that he would play a part in Silva's transfer, asserting the fact that he would never convince Silva to leave.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> Milan chairman <a href="/wiki/Silvio_Berlusconi" title="Silvio Berlusconi">Silvio Berlusconi</a> mentioned a potential transfer on 13 June, saying that Silva needed to be sold for €46 million in order to balance the club's accounts.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> The next day, however, Berlusconi confirmed that Silva would be staying at Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> Transfer news slowed down, and on 2 July, Milan extended Silva's contract to 2017,<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> yet just 12 days later, Silva's transfer to PSG was confirmed.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> The transfer fee was rumoured to be around €42 million, which would have made Silva the most expensive defender in football history.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> Silva had repeatedly stressed the fact that he never pushed for a transfer, and that he was happy at Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> Silva even mentioned that he would like to return to Milan later in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2012.E2.80.9313_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2012–13_season">2012–13 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2012–13 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kiev-PSG_(10).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/52/Kiev-PSG_%2810%29.jpg/220px-Kiev-PSG_%2810%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="448" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/52/Kiev-PSG_%2810%29.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="311" data-file-height="634" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kiev-PSG_(10).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Silva playing for Paris Saint-Germain in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>At his arrival, Silva was presented to the media as the "best defender in the world" by PSG president <a href="/wiki/Nasser_Al-Khelaifi" title="Nasser Al-Khelaifi">Nasser Al-Khelaifi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Then PSG coach, and his former coach with Milan, Carlo Ancelotti, admitted to French media that Silva came to the club injured, and would not be able to participate immediately in matches.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Thirteen days later, Silva was declared fit to play, in time for a <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League group stage">group stage</a> match against <a href="/wiki/FC_Dynamo_Kyiv" title="FC Dynamo Kyiv">Dynamo Kyiv</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> On his debut, Silva scored the second goal in PSG's 4–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> He played his first <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> match against <a href="/wiki/SC_Bastia" title="SC Bastia">Bastia</a>, which PSG dominated, winning 4–0.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October, Silva was played as a central midfielder in PSG's 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_Reims" title="Stade de Reims">Reims</a>; Silva was commended for his display by teammate <a href="/wiki/Salvatore_Sirigu" title="Salvatore Sirigu">Salvatore Sirigu</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> Silva scored his second goal for the club in <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Classique" title="Le Classique">Le Classique</a></i> — the derby between PSG and Marseille.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> He was praised for his defensive display in the match.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> On 16 December, Silva was praised for shackling <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a> forward <a href="/wiki/Lisandro_L%C3%B3pez" title="Lisandro López">Lisandro López</a> in PSG's 1–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> For the 2012 football year, Silva was inducted into the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Silva's first match after the winter break, he was injured in a 0–0 draw against <a href="/wiki/AC_Ajaccio" title="AC Ajaccio">Ajaccio</a>; the MRI confirmed damage to his left bicep, and Silva's recovery time was listed at three weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> It was found that Silva's injury was more serious than initially diagnosed,<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup> and as a result Silva was actually inactive for almost two months.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> Silva made his return in the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Paris_Saint-Germain_v_Valencia" title="2012–13 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League Round of 16</a> against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>. Silva was outstanding in this match, being lauded heavily in France for an "extraterrestrial effort" against the Spanish side.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> In PSG's 1–0 victory over reigning champions <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a>, Silva was regarded as the man of the match with a flawless defensive display.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup> Silva received the <a href="/wiki/UNFP_Player_of_the_Month" title="UNFP Player of the Month">Ligue 1 Player of the Month</a> award for March, with 71% of the vote, after several fantastic performances.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> This was followed by a unanimously-exalted performance against Barcelona, where Silva was described as "a wall" by French and Catalan media.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup> Carlo Ancelotti claimed after the match that Silva was the best defender in the world, saying that Silva had all the ability to win the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Ballon_d%27Or" title="FIFA Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> PSG legend <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Gomes" title="Ricardo Gomes">Ricardo Gomes</a> claimed that Silva was one of Brazil's best-ever defenders, as well as saying that Silva was the best defender in the history of the club.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup> In the return leg, Silva was again praised by Catalan media for a world-class performance.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatleft" style="width:45%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He is the Messi of defenders. The question is no longer if he is the best defender in the world, because he is quite simply one of the best players in the world — better than Cannavaro when he won the Ballon d'Or."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Alain_Roche" title="Alain Roche">Alain Roche</a>, 2013<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Silva continued his run of great performances in PSG's tight 1–0 victory against <a href="/wiki/Troyes_AC" title="Troyes AC">Troyes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> Silva's season came to an end on 5 May when he received a straight red-card in a match against <a href="/wiki/Valenciennes_FC" title="Valenciennes FC">Valenciennes</a>. He motioned to the referee, and put his hands on the referee's shoulder, which the referee deemed as a red-card offence. It was deemed to be a very harsh decision,<sup id="cite_ref-leparisien.fr_158-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-leparisien.fr-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> with former referee <a href="/wiki/Alain_Sars" title="Alain Sars">Alain Sars</a> claiming the expulsion was severe.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> Sporting director Leonardo said that the expulsion was "unacceptable", and Ancelotti said that he did not understand the reason for the expulsion.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> Nevertheless, at the end of the season Silva was voted into the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#2013" title="Trophées UNFP du football">2012–13 Ligue 1 Team of the Year</a> for his level of play throughout the season.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> Silva was also shortlisted for the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a> award, alongside teammates <a href="/wiki/Blaise_Matuidi" title="Blaise Matuidi">Blaise Matuidi</a> and Zlatan Ibrahimovi.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> Over the course of the season, Silva committed an extremely-low 14 fouls, which was mentioned as an excellent total for a defender in <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Parisien" title="Le Parisien">Le Parisien</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-leparisien.fr_158-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-leparisien.fr-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> Silva was considered the best defender in <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> by <i>France Football</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14_season">2013–14 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: 2013–14 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva's season began with a 2–1 victory in the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="Trophée des Champions">French Supercup</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Girondins_de_Bordeaux" title="FC Girondins de Bordeaux">Bordeaux</a>; Silva was voted as man of the match for his display.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> It was the first time Paris Saint-Germain had won the trophy since 1998.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> On 22 August 2013, it was announced that Silva had signed a one-year extension to his contract, keeping him at the club until 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup> In the rematch with Bordeaux at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_Chaban-Delmas" title="Stade Chaban-Delmas">Stade Chaban-Delmas</a>, Silva put in another good performance as PSG won 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> Silva was forced off the field in the 16th minute against <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> due to a left hamstring injury, which ultimately kept him out for six weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> Coming back from his injury, Silva played extremely well against <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>, out-dueling the league's second top-scorer, <a href="/wiki/Dar%C3%ADo_Cvitanich" title="Darío Cvitanich">Darío Cvitanich</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup> Silva had an unusual run of scoring form, netting three times in seven matches. Silva scored in PSG's 4–0 victory over Lyon,<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> 5–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">Sochaux</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> and 4–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Nantes" title="FC Nantes">Nantes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/France_Football" title="France Football">France Football</a></i> rated Silva as the best central defender in Ligue 1 at the half-way point of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the 2013 football year, Silva was inducted into the 2013 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> for the third consecutive year,<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> making him joint-fifth in all-time appearances. Silva was also voted by his fellow professionals in the 2013 <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#Winners" title="FIFPro">FIFPro Team of the Year</a> for the first time in his career.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 January 2014, Manchester United central defender <a href="/wiki/Rio_Ferdinand" title="Rio Ferdinand">Rio Ferdinand</a> claimed that Silva was, by a distance, the best defender in the world.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> Silva was imperious in PSG's 2–0 win against Bordeaux at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a>, where he covered for the errors of teammate <a href="/wiki/Gregory_van_der_Wiel" title="Gregory van der Wiel">Gregory van der Wiel</a> and was even close to scoring himself.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> This performance was followed by another strong performance against Monaco; despite scoring an unlucky own-goal, Silva made crucial interventions throughout the match, including a last-man block against striker <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Rivi%C3%A8re" title="Emmanuel Rivière">Emmanuel Rivière</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> In PSG's comprehensive 4–0 win in the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> over <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a>, Silva was regarded by <i>Le Parisien</i> as having "dominated" then <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> leading-scorer <a href="/wiki/Stefan_Kie%C3%9Fling" title="Stefan Kießling">Stefan Kießling</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup> Marseille defender <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Mendes_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Lucas Mendes (Brazilian footballer)">Lucas Mendes</a> said that Silva was the best defender in the world, and that Silva was his role model as a footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-180" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup> On 16 February, <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, the three-time <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a>, compared the qualities of Silva to legendary German sweeper <a href="/wiki/Franz_Beckenbauer" title="Franz Beckenbauer">Franz Beckenbauer</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup> Silva managed another accomplished display in <i>Le Classique</i>, marshaling the club's defence to a clean sheet and helping extend its lead to eight points at the top of the Ligue 1 table.<sup id="cite_ref-182" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-182">&#91;182&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:35%; ;"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1012376600"/>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"Thiago Silva is without doubt the best central defender in the world. He has incredible qualities. He is a symbol of elegance like Franz Beckenbauer was. Silva follows in his footsteps."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, 2014<sup id="cite_ref-183" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-183">&#91;183&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Quarter-finals" title="2013–14 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">Champions League quarter-finals</a> against <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, Silva conceded his first penalty in over three years, but recovered well in the 3–1 first leg victory<sup id="cite_ref-184" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-184">&#91;184&#93;</a></sup> — Silva's overall defensive effort was well-recognised by both English and French media.<sup id="cite_ref-185" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-185">&#91;185&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-186" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-186">&#91;186&#93;</a></sup> In the second-leg, however, Chelsea prevailed on away goals after a late goal from substitute <a href="/wiki/Demba_Ba" title="Demba Ba">Demba Ba</a>. On 19 April, Silva captained PSG to a 2–1 victory in the <a href="/wiki/2014_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2014 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2014 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>, the first time the club had won the competition since 1998.<sup id="cite_ref-187" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-187">&#91;187&#93;</a></sup> Despite losing 1–2 to <a href="/wiki/Stade_Rennais_F.C." title="Stade Rennais F.C.">Rennes</a>, PSG clinched the league title; Silva had captained the club to their second consecutive league title, and their first double.<sup id="cite_ref-188" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-188">&#91;188&#93;</a></sup> Silva again was shortlisted for <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-189" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-189">&#91;189&#93;</a></sup> and named in the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Team_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Team of the Year</a> for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-190" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-190">&#91;190&#93;</a></sup> Silva was rated by <i>France Football</i> as the league's fifth-best player, as well as the best defender in Ligue 1.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15_season">2014–15 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2014–15 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Silva's season began poorly in PSG's 2–2 draw with Reims; he was rated as one of PSG's worst players in his first match back from the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-191" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-191">&#91;191&#93;</a></sup> In his post-match interview, Silva mentioned how he was not fully fit and that he was finding it difficult to forget Brazil's <a href="/wiki/Mineirazo" class="mw-redirect" title="Mineirazo">embarrassing loss to Germany</a>, where Brazil capitulated without him.<sup id="cite_ref-192" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-192">&#91;192&#93;</a></sup> Only three days after the match against Reims, Silva's rush to get back to full fitness was halted as he suffered a serious thigh injury in a friendly against Napoli on 11 August; he only lasted 13 minutes before being carried off the pitch.<sup id="cite_ref-193" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-193">&#91;193&#93;</a></sup> After nine weeks, Silva was finally pronounced fit on 16 October by manager <a href="/wiki/Laurent_Blanc" title="Laurent Blanc">Laurent Blanc</a>, who also said that Silva would be able to start the next league match against Bordeaux.<sup id="cite_ref-194" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-194">&#91;194&#93;</a></sup> In his return, he had an excellent display alongside fellow countryman <a href="/wiki/David_Luiz" title="David Luiz">David Luiz</a> as PSG dominated Bordeaux, winning 3–0.<sup id="cite_ref-195" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-195">&#91;195&#93;</a></sup> A third of the way into the season, it was observed that Silva's performances were marked with inconsistency, especially throughout November and December. After PSG's 1–3 loss to Barcelona in December, he was criticised by former PSG player <a href="/wiki/Pierre_Ducrocq" title="Pierre Ducrocq">Pierre Ducrocq</a>, who argued that Silva did not have any physical or technical problems, but instead a mentality issue.<sup id="cite_ref-196" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-196">&#91;196&#93;</a></sup> Despite his struggles, Silva was recognised by his peers as being one of the two best central defenders in the world, as he was voted into the <a href="/wiki/FIFPro#FIFA_FIFPro_World_XI" title="FIFPro">2015 FIFPro World XI</a> for the second consecutive year.<sup id="cite_ref-197" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-197">&#91;197&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The 2015 calendar year began extremely well for Silva, with a man of the match display against <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a> in a 1–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-198" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-198">&#91;198&#93;</a></sup> It was followed by another man of the match performance, this time in a 1–0 win against Rennes.<sup id="cite_ref-199" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-199">&#91;199&#93;</a></sup> After the match, Rennes captain <a href="/wiki/Sylvain_Armand" title="Sylvain Armand">Sylvain Armand</a> had nothing but praise for Silva, saying "he [Silva] is a monster and a phenomenon".<sup id="cite_ref-200" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-200">&#91;200&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, Silva was voted as man of the match in PSG's 1–0 <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-201" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-201">&#91;201&#93;</a></sup> Silva's return to form was evident and it met praise from across the country — Pierre Ménès of <i>L'Équipe</i> offered his praise, while Alain Roche of <i>Le Parisien</i> stated that he was back to his best.<sup id="cite_ref-202" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-202">&#91;202&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-203" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-203">&#91;203&#93;</a></sup> After PSG's 1–1 draw with Chelsea in the first leg of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#First_leg" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">2014–15 Champions League Round of 16</a>, Silva was unanimously praised by the French press for his outstanding defensive showing as he marked-out striker <a href="/wiki/Diego_Costa" title="Diego Costa">Diego Costa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-204" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-204">&#91;204&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-205" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-205">&#91;205&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-206" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-206">&#91;206&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he was voted man of the match as he scored his first goal of the season in a 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Toulouse_FC" title="Toulouse FC">Toulouse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-207" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-207">&#91;207&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><i>L'Équipe</i> recognised Silva's incredible performances in January and February with a detailed analysis of his performances — in 2015, Silva was winning 89% of his duels, best in Ligue 1; Silva had 2.9 interceptions, 3.4 tackles, and 7.6 clearances per match, best in Ligue 1; lastly, Silva had committed a remarkable 0 fouls in 630 minutes of play.<sup id="cite_ref-208" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-208">&#91;208&#93;</a></sup> In a 2–0 win against Monaco in the <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a> quarterfinal, Silva was praised for his dominance: one publication noted, "if you thought <a href="/wiki/Dimitar_Berbatov" title="Dimitar Berbatov">Dimitar Berbatov</a> [of Monaco] was silent and invisible throughout the match, it was only due to the work of the Monster".<sup id="cite_ref-209" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-209">&#91;209&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#First_leg" title="2014–15 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">2014–15 Champions League Round of 16</a>, Silva conceded a controversial penalty in the 96th minute. PSG were poised to be eliminated from the Champions League but in the 114th minute, Silva atoned for his error with a towering header to beat <a href="/wiki/Thibaut_Courtois" title="Thibaut Courtois">Thibaut Courtois</a> to help PSG advance to the next stage. Silva was voted by several media sources as the best player in the match as he produced an extraordinary performance.<sup id="cite_ref-210" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-210">&#91;210&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-211" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-211">&#91;211&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-212" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-212">&#91;212&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_2_PSG_0_(13787189375).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg/220px-Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="220" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg/330px-Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/90/Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg/440px-Chelsea_2_PSG_0_%2813787189375%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3456" data-file-height="3456" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Chelsea_2_PSG_0_(13787189375).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Thiago Silva in action for PSG in 2014</div></div></div>
<p>PSG finally took pole position in the league after their 2–3 win over Marseille; Silva was dominant in his duels and played a crucial role in the victory.<sup id="cite_ref-213" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-213">&#91;213&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he was voted man of the match in a 4–1 victory against Saint-Étienne in the Coupe de France semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-214" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-214">&#91;214&#93;</a></sup> On 11 April, Silva captained the club to a 4–0 win in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2015 Coupe de la Ligue Final">Coupe de la Ligue final</a> against Bastia.<sup id="cite_ref-215" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-215">&#91;215&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, Silva suffered an injury in the 20th minute of PSG's quarterfinal against Barcelona.<sup id="cite_ref-216" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-216">&#91;216&#93;</a></sup> He was ruled out for two weeks as PSG were comprehensively beaten 1–5 on aggregate by Barça.<sup id="cite_ref-217" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-217">&#91;217&#93;</a></sup> Upon his return in a 3–1 win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a>, Silva had a comfortable performance as PSG moved closer to the title.<sup id="cite_ref-218" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-218">&#91;218&#93;</a></sup> After an incredible 6–0 win against <a href="/wiki/En_Avant_de_Guingamp" class="mw-redirect" title="En Avant de Guingamp">Guingamp</a> which edged the club closer to the first possible French domestic treble, Silva claimed that this PSG side was the best he had ever played in.<sup id="cite_ref-219" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-219">&#91;219&#93;</a></sup> One week later, PSG clinched the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Ligue_1" title="2014–15 Ligue 1">Ligue 1 title</a> in a hard-fought 2–1 away win at Montpellier; Silva was voted man of the match and he was hailed for marking out <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Barrios" title="Lucas Barrios">Lucas Barrios</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-220" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-220">&#91;220&#93;</a></sup> In the final match of the season, Silva was rated as the best player on the pitch in PSG's 3–2 win against Reims.<sup id="cite_ref-221" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-221">&#91;221&#93;</a></sup> For the third consecutive season, Silva was voted by his peers into the <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Team_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-222" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-222">&#91;222&#93;</a></sup> Silva was also selected in Opta's Ligue 1 Team of the Season based on statistical merit.<sup id="cite_ref-223" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-223">&#91;223&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2015–16 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After playing in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a>, Silva finally returned to club training on 20 July in <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">New Jersey</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-224" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-224">&#91;224&#93;</a></sup> The first pre-season match that Silva played in was the final match of the <a href="/wiki/2015_International_Champions_Cup" title="2015 International Champions Cup">2015 International Champions Cup</a> against Manchester United, where PSG won 2–0 to win the trophy; Silva was rated as the best player in the match.<sup id="cite_ref-225" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-225">&#91;225&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-226" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-226">&#91;226&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, Silva captained PSG to a 2–0 victory in the <a href="/wiki/2015_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2015 Trophée des Champions">2015 Trophée des Champions</a> against Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-227" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-227">&#91;227&#93;</a></sup> Silva had a good match with little to do defensively, as Lyon's star striker <a href="/wiki/Alexandre_Lacazette" title="Alexandre Lacazette">Alexandre Lacazette</a> played an insignificant role in the match.<sup id="cite_ref-228" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-228">&#91;228&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-229" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-229">&#91;229&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>PSG began their <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Ligue_1" title="2015–16 Ligue 1">league campaign</a> with a 1–0 victory against Lille, playing with ten-men for two-thirds of the match.<sup id="cite_ref-230" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-230">&#91;230&#93;</a></sup> Silva had a superb display, leading the defence to a hard-fought clean sheet. His performance was described as dominant, showcasing his intelligence and athleticism throughout the match.<sup id="cite_ref-231" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-231">&#91;231&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
