<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9319_seasons"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–19_seasons">2016–19 seasons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2016–19 seasons">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 8 May 2018, he played as PSG won 2–0 against <a href="/wiki/Les_Herbiers_VF" title="Les Herbiers VF">Les Herbiers VF</a> to clinch the 2017–18 <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-232" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-232">&#91;232&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In April 2020, PSG were awarded the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Ligue_1" title="2019–20 Ligue 1">2019–20 Ligue 1</a> title after the season was ended prematurely due to the outbreak of the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic" title="COVID-19 pandemic">COVID-19 pandemic</a>; at the time of the League's suspension, PSG were in first place, with a twelve–point lead over second–placed Marseille. This was Silva's record seventh Ligue 1 title with the club, which saw him equal the all–time individual record of most Ligue 1 title victories, along with his club teammate <a href="/wiki/Marco_Verratti" title="Marco Verratti">Marco Verratti</a>, which was jointly held by <a href="/wiki/Herv%C3%A9_Revelli" title="Hervé Revelli">Hervé Revelli</a> and <a href="/wiki/Jean-Michel_Larqu%C3%A9" title="Jean-Michel Larqué">Jean-Michel Larqué</a> of Saint-Étienne, as well as <a href="/wiki/Gr%C3%A9gory_Coupet" title="Grégory Coupet">Grégory Coupet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Juninho_Pernambucano" title="Juninho Pernambucano">Juninho</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sidney_Govou" title="Sidney Govou">Sidney Govou</a> of Lyon.<sup id="cite_ref-233" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-233">&#91;233&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-seventh_heaven_234-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-seventh_heaven-234">&#91;234&#93;</a></sup> On 13 June, PSG's sporting director Leonardo reavealed that Thiago Silva would be leaving the club at the end of the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">Champions League campaign</a> in August, alongside his teammate <a href="/wiki/Edinson_Cavani" title="Edinson Cavani">Edinson Cavani</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-235" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-235">&#91;235&#93;</a></sup> PSG completed a domestic treble,<sup id="cite_ref-236" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-236">&#91;236&#93;</a></sup> while his last competitive match for PSG was the <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">2020 UEFA Champions League Final</a> on 23 August, which PSG lost 1–0 to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-237" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-237">&#91;237&#93;</a></sup> However, Silva became the first Brazilian to start a Champions League Final as a captain.<sup id="cite_ref-238" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-238">&#91;238&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chelsea">Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 28 August 2020, Silva joined <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> on a one-year deal with an option for a second.<sup id="cite_ref-239" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-239">&#91;239&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut with the club on 23 September, in a 6–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/Barnsley_F.C." title="Barnsley F.C.">Barnsley</a> in the third round of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_EFL_Cup" title="2020–21 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-240" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-240">&#91;240&#93;</a></sup> Three days later on 26 September, Silva made his Premier League debut in a 3–3 draw against <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a> at <a href="/wiki/The_Hawthorns" title="The Hawthorns">The Hawthorns</a> as captain.<sup id="cite_ref-241" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-241">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup> On 7 November 2020, Silva scored his first goal for Chelsea in a 4–1 home league win over <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_United_F.C." title="Sheffield United F.C.">Sheffield United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-242" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-242">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career_and_2008_Olympics">Early career and 2008 Olympics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Early career and 2008 Olympics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r978413945/mw-parser-output/.tmulti">.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbinner{display:flex;flex-direction:column}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .theader{clear:both;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;align-self:center;background-color:transparent;width:100%}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .thumbcaption{background-color:transparent}.mw-parser-output .thumbcaption{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .tmulti .trow>.thumbcaption{text-align:center}}</style><div class="thumb tmulti tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:314px;max-width:314px"><div class="trow"><div class="tsingle" style="width:160px;max-width:160px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_Silva_Brazil-England_2009.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fe/Thiago_Silva_Brazil-England_2009.jpg/158px-Thiago_Silva_Brazil-England_2009.jpg" decoding="async" width="158" height="272" class="thumbcaption">Thiago Silva playing for <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>, on 14 November 2009.</div></div><div class="tsingle" style="width:150px;max-width:150px"><div class="thumbimage"><a href="/wiki/File:Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg/148px-Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg" decoding="async" width="148" height="272" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg/222px-Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg/296px-Thiago_Silva_-_Brazil_2011.jpg 2x" data-file-width="825" data-file-height="1516" /></a></div><div class="thumbcaption">Thiago Silva in a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Scotland_national_football_team" title="Scotland national football team">Scotland</a>, on 27 March 2011.</div></div></div></div></div>
<p>After a strong season with Fluminense, Silva was called up to the <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> preliminary squad for the <a href="/wiki/2007_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2007 Copa América">2007 Copa América</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-243" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-243">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup> though he was not a part of the main team which ultimately won the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-244" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-244">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup> Silva was then called up for a friendly against <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> on 15 August,<sup id="cite_ref-245" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-245">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup> failing to leave the bench, as Brazil won 2–0.<sup id="cite_ref-246" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-246">&#91;246&#93;</a></sup> Silva was then selected by <a href="/wiki/Dunga" title="Dunga">Dunga</a> to play in the <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Olympics" title="2008 Summer Olympics">2008 Summer Olympics</a>, one of two overage players, alongside <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a>. Silva won his first two caps for Brazil in pre-Olympic friendlies against <a href="/wiki/Singapore_national_football_team" title="Singapore national football team">Singapore</a> and <a href="/wiki/Vietnam_national_football_team" title="Vietnam national football team">Vietnam</a>, though he suffered a right calf injury against Vietnam that kept him out of Brazil's first Olympic match.<sup id="cite_ref-247" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-247">&#91;247&#93;</a></sup> He was finally pronounced fit for the third group match, where Silva started and Brazil won 3–0 against <a href="/wiki/China_national_football_team" title="China national football team">China</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-248" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-248">&#91;248&#93;</a></sup> He did not start any other matches, only coming on in the 71st minute against <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> in the third-place match, which sealed the bronze medal for Brazil.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;249&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva's next cap came in an international friendly against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> on 20 November 2008; Brazil won by a convincing 6–2 scoreline,<sup id="cite_ref-250" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-250">&#91;250&#93;</a></sup> and Silva was praised for having "dominated" the reigning <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Player_of_the_Year" title="FIFA World Player of the Year">FIFA World Player of the Year</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">&#91;251&#93;</a></sup> Silva was praised by his teammates for his performance.<sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;252&#93;</a></sup> He was not a starter during the <a href="/wiki/2010_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2010 FIFA World Cup">2010 FIFA World Cup</a> cycle for Brazil, despite his high level of club performances for Milan.<sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;253&#93;</a></sup> He was still playing in friendly matches, and in a November 2009 friendly against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>, Silva put in a man of the match display in <a href="/wiki/Doha" title="Doha">Doha</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-254" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-254">&#91;254&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2010_World_Cup_and_2011_Copa_América">2010 World Cup and 2011 Copa América</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: 2010 World Cup and 2011 Copa América">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva was an unused substitute in all matches at the 2010 World Cup, where Brazil were defeated in the quarter-finals by the eventual finalists, the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-255" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-255">&#91;255&#93;</a></sup> Silva was selected as captain by new Brazil coach <a href="/wiki/Mano_Menezes" title="Mano Menezes">Mano Menezes</a> ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONMEBOL)" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONMEBOL)">2014 World Cup qualifying cycle</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/L%C3%BAcio" title="Lúcio">Lúcio</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-256" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-256">&#91;256&#93;</a></sup> Brazil disappointed at the <a href="/wiki/2011_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2011 Copa América">2011 Copa América</a>, losing in a penalty shootout to <a href="/wiki/Paraguay_national_football_team" title="Paraguay national football team">Paraguay</a>, where every Brazilian player — <a href="/wiki/Fred_(footballer,_born_1983)" title="Fred (footballer, born 1983)">Fred</a>, <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9_Santos" title="André Santos">André Santos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Elano" title="Elano">Elano</a> and Silva — failed to convert their penalties in shocking fashion.<sup id="cite_ref-257" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-257">&#91;257&#93;</a></sup> Silva scored his first goal for Brazil in an friendly match against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national soccer team">United States</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-258" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-258">&#91;258&#93;</a></sup> International honours still eluded Silva at the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_2012_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 2012 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">2012 Summer Olympics</a>, as <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_football_team" title="Mexico national football team">Mexico</a> surprised Brazil in the final to win 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-259" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-259">&#91;259&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2013_Confederations_Cup">2013 Confederations Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 2013 Confederations Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Silva's first international trophy came at the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIFA_Confederations_Cup" title="2013 FIFA Confederations Cup">2013 FIFA Confederations Cup</a>, held in Brazil. As a warm-up tournament to the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 World Cup</a>, the Brazilian side dominated all opposition, winning the tournament with an overall aggregate score of 14–3.<sup id="cite_ref-260" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-260">&#91;260&#93;</a></sup> Silva was outstanding throughout the tournament; he was rated as the tenth-best player at the end of the group stages,<sup id="cite_ref-261" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-261">&#91;261&#93;</a></sup> and by the end of the tournament, he was rated as the fifth-best player of the tournament by the <a href="/wiki/Castrol_Performance_Index" class="mw-redirect" title="Castrol Performance Index">Castrol Performance Index</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-262" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-262">&#91;262&#93;</a></sup> Silva was also voted into the Confederations Cup Dream Team by FIFA.com users.<sup id="cite_ref-Dream_Team_263-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Dream_Team-263">&#91;263&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva scored his second goal for Brazil in a 3–1 friendly victory over Portugal on 11 September 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-264" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-264">&#91;264&#93;</a></sup> In a pre-World Cup friendly against <a href="/wiki/Serbia_national_football_team" title="Serbia national football team">Serbia</a>, Silva assisted Fred's goal as Brazil ran out with a 1–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-265" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-265">&#91;265&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_World_Cup">2014 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 2014 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_(3).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg/220px-Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="254" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg/330px-Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg/440px-Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_%283%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="867" data-file-height="1000" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Brazil_and_Colombia_match_at_the_FIFA_World_Cup_2014-07-04_(3).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Thiago Silva celebrating Brazil's victory against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a> at the 2014 World Cup.</div></div></div>
<p>With Silva playing for the first time at a <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a>, Brazil won 3–1 against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a> in their first match at the 2014 World Cup, held on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-266" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-266">&#91;266&#93;</a></sup> Silva was regarded as Brazil's best player in their second match, a 0–0 draw against Mexico,<sup id="cite_ref-267" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-267">&#91;267&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-268" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-268">&#91;268&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-269" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-269">&#91;269&#93;</a></sup> making several crucial interventions and getting involved offensively.<sup id="cite_ref-270" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-270">&#91;270&#93;</a></sup> In the final group match against <a href="/wiki/Cameroon_national_football_team" title="Cameroon national football team">Cameroon</a>, Silva was again outstanding as Brazil won by a decisive 4–1 scoreline.<sup id="cite_ref-271" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-271">&#91;271&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-272" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-272">&#91;272&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the group stage, <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> rated Silva as the third-best defender of the tournament, and the ninth-best player overall.<sup id="cite_ref-273" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-273">&#91;273&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In Brazil's victory over <a href="/wiki/Chile_national_football_team" title="Chile national football team">Chile</a> in the round of 16, Silva assisted the opening goal scored by <a href="/wiki/David_Luiz" title="David Luiz">David Luiz</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-274" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-274">&#91;274&#93;</a></sup> Chile equalised, and after no goals were scored in extra-time, the match went to a penalty shootout. Silva faced severe criticism for his behaviour, as he was pictured in tears before and during the shootout.<sup id="cite_ref-275" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-275">&#91;275&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/1970_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1970 FIFA World Cup">1970 World Cup</a>-winning captain <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Alberto_Torres" title="Carlos Alberto Torres">Carlos Alberto</a> asserted that Silva was a weak captain, while Brazilian legend <a href="/wiki/Zico_(footballer)" title="Zico (footballer)">Zico</a> insisted that Silva should have volunteered to take a penalty, instead of refusing to take one.<sup id="cite_ref-276" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-276">&#91;276&#93;</a></sup> After the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup#Round_of_16" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">Round of 16</a>, Silva was still regarded as one of the best defenders of the tournament by multiple media sources.<sup id="cite_ref-277" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-277">&#91;277&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-278" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-278">&#91;278&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was able to silence his critics by scoring the opening goal in the quarterfinal against <a href="/wiki/Colombia_national_football_team" title="Colombia national football team">Colombia</a>, and was seen as a top performer in the match;<sup id="cite_ref-279" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-279">&#91;279&#93;</a></sup> however, Silva picked up his second yellow card of the tournament for obstructing goalkeeper <a href="/wiki/David_Ospina" title="David Ospina">David Ospina</a>, which ruled him out of the semi-final.<sup id="cite_ref-280" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-280">&#91;280&#93;</a></sup> Brazil tried to appeal his yellow card,<sup id="cite_ref-281" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-281">&#91;281&#93;</a></sup> but it was immediately rejected.<sup id="cite_ref-282" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-282">&#91;282&#93;</a></sup> Nevertheless, at the end of the quarter-final stage, Silva was rated by FIFA as the second-best defender of the tournament, and the fourth-best player overall.<sup id="cite_ref-283" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-283">&#91;283&#93;</a></sup> Silva's suspension brought apprehension to the team; <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a> even claimed that Silva was Brazil's most important player, praising the stability Silva offers to the defence.<sup id="cite_ref-284" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-284">&#91;284&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva was replaced by <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> defender <a href="/wiki/Dante_(footballer)" title="Dante (footballer)">Dante</a>, who was deemed by <a href="/wiki/Germany_national_football_team" title="Germany national football team">Germany</a> coach <a href="/wiki/Joachim_L%C3%B6w" title="Joachim Löw">Joachim Löw</a> as "an excellent player".<sup id="cite_ref-285" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-285">&#91;285&#93;</a></sup> Without Silva as captain, Brazil capitulated in the semi-final, losing by a record <a href="/wiki/Brazil_v_Germany_(2014_FIFA_World_Cup)" title="Brazil v Germany (2014 FIFA World Cup)">1–7 scoreline to Germany</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-286" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-286">&#91;286&#93;</a></sup> It was widely recognised that Silva's absence played a crucial part in the shock result.<sup id="cite_ref-287" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-287">&#91;287&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-288" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-288">&#91;288&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-289" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-289">&#91;289&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-290" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-290">&#91;290&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the third-place match, Silva returned, but his presence could not salvage any honours for Brazil, as they were comprehensively beaten 3–0 by the Netherlands. In the second minute of the game, Silva pulled down <a href="/wiki/Arjen_Robben" title="Arjen Robben">Arjen Robben</a>, as he ran into <a href="/wiki/J%C3%BAlio_C%C3%A9sar_(footballer,_born_1986)" title="Júlio César (footballer, born 1986)">Júlio César</a>'s box with the ball for a clear goal-scoring opportunity. Under FIFA rules Silva ought to have been shown a red card, but he was shown a yellow card instead by the Algerian referee <a href="/wiki/Djamel_Haimoudi" title="Djamel Haimoudi">Djamel Haimoudi</a>. The referee called for a penalty, while the foul happened outside the box, which was successfully scored by <a href="/wiki/Robin_van_Persie" title="Robin van Persie">Robin van Persie</a>.
</p><p>At the conclusion of the tournament, Silva was rated by FIFA as the third-best central defender, and the eighth-best player overall.<sup id="cite_ref-291" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-291">&#91;291&#93;</a></sup> Silva was selected into the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#All-Star_Team" title="FIFA World Cup awards">FIFA World Cup Dream Team</a> voted by FIFA.com users,<sup id="cite_ref-292" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-292">&#91;292&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Castrol_Performance_Index" class="mw-redirect" title="Castrol Performance Index">Castrol World Cup Top XI</a> based on statistical merit.<sup id="cite_ref-Castrol_Index_Top_11_293-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Castrol_Index_Top_11-293">&#91;293&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2015_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015_Copa_América">2015 Copa América</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 2015 Copa América">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Brazil, under Dunga's second stint as manager, went to the <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2015 Copa América">2015 Copa América</a> in Chile with <a href="/wiki/Neymar" title="Neymar">Neymar</a> as the captain. After his suspension for the remainder of the tournament in their second game, however, the armband did not go back to Silva, but rather to his defensive partner, <a href="/wiki/Miranda_(footballer,_born_1984)" title="Miranda (footballer, born 1984)">Miranda</a>. In Brazil's final <a href="/wiki/2015_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Group_C" title="2015 Copa América Group C">group</a> match against <a href="/wiki/Venezuela_national_football_team" title="Venezuela national football team">Venezuela</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Monumental_David_Arellano" title="Estadio Monumental David Arellano">Estadio Monumental David Arellano</a> in <a href="/wiki/Santiago" title="Santiago">Santiago</a>, Silva opened the scoring in the ninth minute, volleying in a corner from <a href="/wiki/Robinho" title="Robinho">Robinho</a>. The eventual 2–1 victory sent Brazil into the quarter-finals as group winners.<sup id="cite_ref-294" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-294">&#91;294&#93;</a></sup> In the 70th minute of the quarter-final, Silva's handball gave Paraguay the penalty kick from which they equalised for a 1–1 draw; Brazil lost in the subsequent <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shootout</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-295" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-295">&#91;295&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_World_Cup">2018 World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 2018 World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 14 May 2018, Silva was named by <a href="/wiki/Tite_(football_manager)" title="Tite (football manager)">Tite</a> in the squad for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-296" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-296">&#91;296&#93;</a></sup> On 27 June 2018, he scored the second goal in Brazil's 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Serbia_national_football_team" title="Serbia national football team">Serbia</a> for the last match of the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-297" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-297">&#91;297&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2019_Copa_Am.C3.A9rica"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019_Copa_América">2019 Copa América</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 2019 Copa América">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In May 2019, he was included in Brazil's 23-man squad for the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica" title="2019 Copa América">2019 Copa América</a> on home soil.<sup id="cite_ref-298" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-298">&#91;298&#93;</a></sup> He started in the <a href="/wiki/2019_Copa_Am%C3%A9rica_Final" title="2019 Copa América Final">final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Peru_national_football_team" title="Peru national football team">Peru</a> on 7 July, at the <a href="/wiki/Maracan%C3%A3_Stadium" title="Maracanã Stadium">Maracanã Stadium</a>; the match ended in a 3–1 victory to Brazil.<sup id="cite_ref-2019_Copa_América_Final_299-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019_Copa_América_Final-299">&#91;299&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Silva has been recognized as a complete defender by his peers and critics. He has been described as a consistent defender, without any flaws, and someone who can lead any defence.<sup id="cite_ref-auto1_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto1-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> A leader from the back, Silva's play has led him to be compared to legendary Italian defender <a href="/wiki/Franco_Baresi" title="Franco Baresi">Franco Baresi</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-300" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-300">&#91;300&#93;</a></sup> Baresi, regarded as one of the greatest defenders in football history,<sup id="cite_ref-301" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-301">&#91;301&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-302" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-302">&#91;302&#93;</a></sup> has gone on record to state that Silva is the defender who most resembles him,<sup id="cite_ref-303" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-303">&#91;303&#93;</a></sup> and said in June 2012 that Silva was his "heir".<sup id="cite_ref-304" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-304">&#91;304&#93;</a></sup> Although he has been criticised at times in the media over his mentality, his leadership skills are also apparent through his success in captaining both Brazil and Paris Saint-Germain.<sup id="cite_ref-305" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-305">&#91;305&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-306" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-306">&#91;306&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-307" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-307">&#91;307&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Silva is heralded as one of the fastest defenders in European football,<sup id="cite_ref-308" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-308">&#91;308&#93;</a></sup> and has been described as a strong defender with good aerial ability.<sup id="cite_ref-CorSportFlu_309-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CorSportFlu-309">&#91;309&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-310" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-310">&#91;310&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-goal.com_311-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal.com-311">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup> He combines these physical gifts with a phenomenal tactical intelligence and knowledge of the game, as well as an excellent positional sense.<sup id="cite_ref-312" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-312">&#91;312&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-CorSport_313-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CorSport-313">&#91;313&#93;</a></sup> Thanks to his abilities, he excels at reading and anticipating plays and is excellent at closing down opposing players in possession of the ball.<sup id="cite_ref-goal.com_311-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goal.com-311">&#91;311&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-GazzettaGerna_314-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GazzettaGerna-314">&#91;314&#93;</a></sup> Hailed as the best of the new breed of defenders<sup id="cite_ref-315" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-315">&#91;315&#93;</a></sup> — composed in possession, able to create chances for his team from the back — Silva is a defender who is universally praised, being voted as one of the top two central defenders in Europe for three consecutive years.<sup id="cite_ref-316" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-316">&#91;316&#93;</a></sup> Despite his ability, however, he has also struggled with injuries throughout his career.<sup id="cite_ref-ultimouomo_317-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ultimouomo-317">&#91;317&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Silva and his wife Isabele have two sons named Isago and Iago.<sup id="cite_ref-318" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-318">&#91;318&#93;</a></sup> Silva is a <a href="/wiki/Christianity" title="Christianity">Christian</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-319" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-319">&#91;319&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-320" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-320">&#91;320&#93;</a></sup> On March 15, 2019 after playing almost seven years in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a> with <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain" class="mw-redirect" title="Paris Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</a>, Thiago announced that he, his wife and children had also become French citizens.<sup id="cite_ref-321" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-321">&#91;321&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Thiago_Silva&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
